# Innovations

> Auto-generated by `scripts/atlas.mjs` on 2026-07-05. Skills that exist in a fork's `skills/` directory but **not** in [`aaronjmars/aeon`](https://github.com/aaronjmars/aeon).

**202** of 204 forks ship at least one custom skill. **263** distinct novel skills across the network.

The atlas reads each fork's git tree (not just `aeon.yml`), so this catches skills that exist in code even when they're not enabled — the actual long tail of code-level innovation in the ecosystem.
